CREATE TABLE `accounitng_period_lock_info` (
  `id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `periodname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `startdate` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `enddate` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `subperiodof` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `periodtype` int(2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `peridclosed` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',
  `artransactionclosed` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',
  `aptransactionclosed` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',
  `allgltransactionclosed` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',
  `company` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `userid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `periodformat` int(2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `yearinperiodname` int(2) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `fk_accounitng_period_lock_info` (`company`),
  KEY `fk_accounitng_period_lock_info_sub_periodof` (`subperiodof`),
  KEY `fk_accounitng_period_lock_info_useid` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `accounitng_period_lock_info_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`userid`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_accounitng_period_lock_info` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_accounitng_period_lock_info_sub_periodof` FOREIGN KEY (`subperiodof`) REFERENCES `accounitng_period_lock_info` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `tdsdetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `documenttype` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `documentid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `documentdetails` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `includetaxamount` int(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  `account` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `ruleid` int(10) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `tdspercentage` double(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tdsamount` double(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `enteramount` double(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `paymentdetail` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `tdsdetails_ibfk_1` (`paymentdetail`),
  KEY `tdsdetails_ibfk_2` (`account`),
  KEY `tdsdetails_ibfk_3` (`ruleid`),
  KEY `tdsdetails_ibfk_4` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `tdsdetails_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`paymentdetail`) REFERENCES `paymentdetail` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `tdsdetails_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`account`) REFERENCES `account` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `tdsdetails_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`ruleid`) REFERENCES `tds_rate` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `tdsdetails_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# Anand Nimbalkar 13 April, 2016
CREATE TABLE `linkdetailreceipttoadvancepayment` (
  `id` varchar(36) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(36) NOT NULL,
  `amount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `receipt` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `paymentid` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `srno` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `fromcurrency` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tocurrency` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `exchangeratefortransaction` double DEFAULT '1',
  `amountinpaymentcurrency` double DEFAULT '1',
  `linkedgainlossje` varchar(40) DEFAULT '',
  `receiptlinkdate` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `revaljeid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `revaljeidreceipt` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `receipt` (`receipt`),
  KEY `company` (`company`),
  KEY `paymentid` (`paymentid`),
  KEY `fromcurrency` (`fromcurrency`),
  KEY `tocurrency` (`tocurrency`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailreceipttoadvancepayment_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`receipt`) REFERENCES `receipt` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailreceipttoadvancepayment_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailreceipttoadvancepayment_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`paymentid`) REFERENCES `payment` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailreceipttoadvancepayment_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`fromcurrency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailreceipttoadvancepayment_ibfk_5` FOREIGN KEY (`tocurrency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `linkdetailpaymenttoadvancepayment` (
  `id` varchar(36) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(36) NOT NULL,
  `amount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `payment` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `receipt` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `srno` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `fromcurrency` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tocurrency` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `exchangeratefortransaction` double DEFAULT '1',
  `amountinpaymentcurrency` double DEFAULT '1',
  `linkedgainlossje` varchar(40) DEFAULT '',
  `paymentlinkdate` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `revaljeid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `revaljeidreceipt` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `receipt` (`receipt`),
  KEY `company` (`company`),
  KEY `payment` (`payment`),
  KEY `fromcurrency` (`fromcurrency`),
  KEY `tocurrency` (`tocurrency`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailpaymenttoadvancepayment_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`receipt`) REFERENCES `receipt` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailpaymenttoadvancepayment_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailpaymenttoadvancepayment_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`payment`) REFERENCES `payment` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailpaymenttoadvancepayment_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`fromcurrency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `linkdetailpaymenttoadvancepayment_ibfk_5` FOREIGN KEY (`tocurrency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `labour` (
`id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`empcode` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`fname` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`lname` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`mname` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`dob` date NOT NULL, 
`age` varchar(50)  DEFAULT NULL,
`gender` varchar(50)  DEFAULT NULL,
`maritalstatus` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`bgroup` varchar(50)  DEFAULT NULL,
`nationality` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`countryorigin` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`keyskill` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`taskassigned` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`shifttiming` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`department` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`dlicenseno` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`passportno` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`expirydatepassport` date  DEFAULT NULL,
`paycycle` varchar(50)  DEFAULT NULL,
`residentstatus` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
`prdate` date  DEFAULT NULL,
`race` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
`religion` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
`bankac` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`bankaname` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`accountname` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`accountnumber` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`banknumber` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`branchnumber` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`bankbranch` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`paymentmethod` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
`company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,  
`deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
`createdby` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
`modifiedby` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
`acclabourcustomdataref` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,  
PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
FOREIGN KEY (`createdby`)  REFERENCES `users`(`userid`),
FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`)  REFERENCES `users`(`userid`),
FOREIGN KEY (`paymentmethod`) REFERENCES `paymentmethod` (`id`))ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `mrpcontract` (
  `id` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  `company` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  `contractid` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contractname` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `customer` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `creationdate` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  `sellertype` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contractstartdate` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  `contractenddate` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  `contractterm` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contractstatus` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `parentcontractid` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `parentcontractname` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleteflag` CHAR(1) NOT NULL,
  #Payment Terms
  `paymentmethodname` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `accountname` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `detailstype` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `autopopulate` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shownincsorcp` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `bankname` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `bankaccountnumber` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `bankaddress` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `paymenttermname` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `paymenttermdays` INT(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `paymenttermdate` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  #Document Required
  `contractorname` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contractorteename` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pannumber` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tannumber` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dateofaggrement` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  `countryaggrement` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `stateaggrement` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `previouscontractid` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `documentrequiredremarks` VARCHAR(1024) DEFAULT NULL,
  `actualattachment` VARCHAR(512) DEFAULT NULL,

  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_company` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_sellertype` (`sellertype`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_contractstatus` (`contractstatus`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_parentcontractid` (`parentcontractid`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_countryaggrement` (`countryaggrement`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_customer` (`customer`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_paymentmethodname` (`paymentmethodname`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontract_paymenttermname` (`paymenttermname`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_sellertype` FOREIGN KEY (`sellertype`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_contractstatus` FOREIGN KEY (`contractstatus`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_parentcontractid` FOREIGN KEY (`parentcontractid`) REFERENCES `mrpcontract` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_countryaggrement` FOREIGN KEY (`countryaggrement`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_customer` FOREIGN KEY (`customer`) REFERENCES `customer` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_paymentmethodname` FOREIGN KEY (`paymentmethodname`) REFERENCES `paymentmethod` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontract_paymenttermname` FOREIGN KEY (`paymenttermname`) REFERENCES `creditterm` (`termid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `mrpcontractdetails` (
  `id` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  `mrpcontract` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  `product` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  `description` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `quantity` INT(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  #Shipment Contract
  `deliverymode` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `totalnoofunit` INT(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `totalquantity` INT(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shippingperiodfrom` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  `shippingperiodto` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  `partialshipmentallowed` INT(5) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipmentstatus` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shippingagent` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `loadingportcountry` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `loadingport` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `transshipmentallowed` INT(5) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dischargeportcountry` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dischargeport` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `finaldestination` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `postalcode` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `budgetfreightcost` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipmentcontractremarks` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `uom` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `basequantity` DOUBLE DEFAULT 0,
  `discount` DOUBLE DEFAULT 0,
  `amount` DOUBLE DEFAULT NULL,
  #Packaging Contract
  `unitweightvalue` INT(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `unitweight` INT(20) DEFAULT 0,
  `packagingtype` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `certificaterequirement` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `certificate` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shippingmarksdetails` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipmentmode` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `percontainerload` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `palletmaterial` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `packagingprofiletype` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `marking` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `drumorbagdetails` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `drumorbagsize` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `numberoflayers` INT(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `heatingpad` INT(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `palletloadcontainer` INT(20) DEFAULT NULL,

  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontractdetails_mrpcontract` (`mrpcontract`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontractdetails_product` (`product`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontractdetails_company` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontractdetails_uom` (`uom`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontractdetails_packagingprofiletype` (`packagingprofiletype`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontractdetails_deliverymode` (`deliverymode`),
  KEY `FK_mrpcontractdetails_shipmentstatus` (`shipmentstatus`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdetails_mrpcontract` FOREIGN KEY (`mrpcontract`) REFERENCES `mrpcontract` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdetails_product` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdetails_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdetails_uom` FOREIGN KEY (`uom`) REFERENCES `uom` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdetails_packagingprofiletype` FOREIGN KEY (`packagingprofiletype`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdetails_deliverymode` FOREIGN KEY (`deliverymode`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdetails_shipmentstatus` FOREIGN KEY (`shipmentstatus`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `mrpaddressdetails` (
  `id` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  `mrpcontractdetails` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `mrpcontract` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `aliasname` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `address` VARCHAR(1024) DEFAULT NULL,
  `city` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `state` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `postalcode` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `mobilenumber` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `fax` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `emailid` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `recipientname` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contactperson` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contactpersonnumber` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `contactpersondesignation` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `website` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `route` VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `isbilling` CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'T',

  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK_mrpaddressdetails_mrpcontractdetails` (`mrpcontractdetails`),
  KEY `FK_mrpaddressdetails_mrpcontract` (`mrpcontract`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpaddressdetails_mrpcontractdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`mrpcontractdetails`) REFERENCES `mrpcontractdetails` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpaddressdetails_mrpcontract` FOREIGN KEY (`mrpcontract`) REFERENCES `mrpcontract` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Vivekanand Swami 23 April, 2016

CREATE TABLE `producttermsmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `product` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `percentage` double DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `account` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `term` (`term`),
  KEY `product` (`product`),
  KEY `account` (`account`),
  CONSTRAINT `producttermsmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `producttermsmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `producttermsmap_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`account`) REFERENCES `account` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Ajit Ankalle 23th April 2016
CREATE TABLE `receiptdetailtermsmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `goodsreceiptdetail` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `term` (`term`),
  KEY `goodsreceiptdetail` (`goodsreceiptdetail`),
  CONSTRAINT `receiptdetailtermsmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `receiptdetailtermsmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`goodsreceiptdetail`) REFERENCES `grdetails` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Sayed Kausar Ali 25 April 2016
CREATE TABLE `workcenter` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `seqformat` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `workcenterid` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `workcentertype` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `workcenterlocation` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `workcentercapacity` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `worktype` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `workcentermanager` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `costcenter` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `createdby` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `modifiedby` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `warehouseid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK_workcenter_seqformat` (`seqformat`),
  KEY `FK_wc_company` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_wc_createdby` (`createdby`),
  KEY `FK_wc_modifiedby` (`modifiedby`),
  KEY `FK_wc_wctype` (`workcentertype`),
  KEY `FK_wc_worktype` (`worktype`),
  KEY `FK_wc_costcenter` (`costcenter`),
  KEY `FK_wc_warehouse` (`warehouseid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_costcenter` FOREIGN KEY (`costcenter`) REFERENCES `costcenter` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_createdby` FOREIGN KEY (`createdby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_modifiedby` FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_warehouse` FOREIGN KEY (`warehouseid`) REFERENCES `inventorywarehouse` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_wctype` FOREIGN KEY (`workcentertype`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_worktype` FOREIGN KEY (`worktype`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_workcenter_seqformat` FOREIGN KEY (`seqformat`) REFERENCES `sequenceformat` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# MRP - Machine Master 
#Dipak Dorkar  25th April, 2016
CREATE TABLE machine (
  id varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  machinename varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  machineid varchar(1024) NOT NULL,
  machineserialno varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  seqnumber int(11) DEFAULT '0',  
  datesuffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '',
  datepreffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '',
  createdon bigint(20) DEFAULT '0',
  machineoperatingcapacity varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  machineusescount double DEFAULT '0',
  dateofinstallation date DEFAULT NULL,
  dateofpurchase date DEFAULT NULL,
  insuranceduedate date DEFAULT NULL,
  machinevendor varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  ageofmachine varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  ismachineonlease char(1) default 'F',
  deleted char(1) default 'F',
  issubstitute char(1) default 'F',
  autogen char(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'F',
  company varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  seqformat varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  purchaseaccount varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  vendor varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_CompanyID FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company(companyid),
  CONSTRAINT fk_Vendor FOREIGN KEY (vendor) REFERENCES vendor (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_PurchaseAccount FOREIGN KEY (purchaseaccount) REFERENCES account(id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_SeqFormat FOREIGN KEY (seqformat) REFERENCES sequenceformat(id)
 ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


CREATE TABLE machine_process_mapping (
  id varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  machineid varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  processid varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  company varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_MachineID FOREIGN KEY (machineid) REFERENCES machine(id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_ProcessID FOREIGN KEY (processid) REFERENCES masteritem (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_compid FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company(companyid)
 ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;





CREATE TABLE substitute_machine_mapping (
  id varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  substitutemachineid varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  activemachineid varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  company varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_Substitute_Machine_ID FOREIGN KEY (substitutemachineid) REFERENCES machine(id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_Active_Machine_ID FOREIGN KEY (activemachineid) REFERENCES machine(id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_Comp_Substitute_id FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company(companyid)
 ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;



CREATE TABLE machine_work_center_mapping (
  id varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  machineid varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  workcenterid varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  company varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_Machine_WC_ID FOREIGN KEY (machineid) REFERENCES machine(id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_Machine_WC_Map_ID FOREIGN KEY (workcenterid) REFERENCES workcenter (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_compa_WC_id FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company(companyid)
 ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `term` varchar(40) NOT NULL,

  `percentage` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` date DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `receiptorderdetailtermsmap_ibfk_1` (`term`),

  CONSTRAINT `receiptorderdetailtermsmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `receiptorderdetailtermsmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`grodetail`) REFERENCES `grodetails` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Sayed kausar Ali 26 Apr 2016

 CREATE TABLE `workorder` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `workordername` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `workorderid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `seqformat` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `salescontractid` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dateofdelivery` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `routecode` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `workordertype` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `workorderstatus` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `salesorder` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `productid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `customer` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `createdby` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `modifiedby` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK_workorder_seqformat` (`seqformat`),
  KEY `FK_wo_productid` (`productid`),
  KEY `FK_wo_salesorder` (`salesorder`),
  KEY `FK_wo_company` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_wo_workordertype` (`workordertype`),
  KEY `FK_wo_workorderstatus` (`workorderstatus`),
  KEY `FK_wo_cutsomer` (`customer`),
  KEY `FK_wo_createdby` (`createdby`),
  KEY `FK_wo_modifiedby` (`modifiedby`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_createdby` FOREIGN KEY (`createdby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_cutsomer` FOREIGN KEY (`customer`) REFERENCES `customer` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_modifiedby` FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_productid` FOREIGN KEY (`productid`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_salesorder` FOREIGN KEY (`salesorder`) REFERENCES `salesorder` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_workorderstatus` FOREIGN KEY (`workorderstatus`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_wo_workordertype` FOREIGN KEY (`workordertype`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_workorder_seqformat` FOREIGN KEY (`seqformat`) REFERENCES `sequenceformat` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ;

CREATE TABLE `mrp_job_order` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `jobordername` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `seqformat` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `jobordernumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `jobworkdate` date NOT NULL,
  `dateofdelivery` date NOT NULL,
  `vendorid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `dateofshipment` date NOT NULL,
  `excisedutychargees` double DEFAULT 0.0,
  `jobworklocation` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `shipmentroute` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `gatepass` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `otherremarks` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `workorderid` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `productid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `productquantity` double NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,
	`deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `creator` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `modifiedby` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `seqnumber` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
datesuffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '',
  datepreffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '',
autogen char(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'F',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK_mrp_job_order_seqformat` (`seqformat`),
  KEY `FK_mrp_job_order_vendorid` (`vendorid`),
  KEY `FK_mrp_job_order_workorder` (`workorderid`),
  KEY `FK_mrp_job_order_productid` (`productid`),
  KEY `FK_mrp_job_order_companyid` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_mrp_job_order_creator` (`creator`),
  KEY `FK_mrp_job_order_modifiedby` (`modifiedby`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrp_job_order_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrp_job_order_creator` FOREIGN KEY (`creator`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrp_job_order_modifiedby` FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrp_job_order_productid` FOREIGN KEY (`productid`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrp_job_order_seqformat` FOREIGN KEY (`seqformat`) REFERENCES `sequenceformat` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrp_job_order_vendorid` FOREIGN KEY (`vendorid`) REFERENCES `vendor` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_mrp_job_order_workorder` FOREIGN KEY (`workorderid`) REFERENCES `workorder` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `createdon` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `salesorderdetailtermmap_ibfk_1` (`term`),
  KEY `salesorderdetailtermmap_ibfk_2` (`salesorderdetail`),
  CONSTRAINT `salesorderdetailtermmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `salesorderdetailtermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`salesorderdetail`) REFERENCES `sodetails` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `salesorderdetailtermproduct` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;



CREATE TABLE `quotationdetailtermmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `quotationdetail` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` double DEFAULT '0',
  `assessablevalue` double DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `quotationdetailtermmap_ibfk_1` (`term`),
  KEY `quotationdetailtermmap_ibfk_2` (`quotationdetail`),
  CONSTRAINT `quotationdetailtermmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `quotationdetailtermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`quotationdetail`) REFERENCES `quotationdetails` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `quotationdetailtermproduct` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `invoicedetailtermsmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `invoicedetail` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `assessablevalue` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `term` (`term`),
  KEY `invoicedetail` (`invoicedetail`),
  CONSTRAINT `invoicedetailtermsmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `invoicedetailtermsmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`invoicedetail`) REFERENCES `invoicedetails` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `purchaseorderdetailstermmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40)  NOT NULL,
  `podetails` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(40)  NOT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` double DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `purchaseorderdetailstermmap_ibfk_1` (`term`),
  KEY `purchaseorderdetailstermmap_ibfk_2` (`podetails`),
  KEY `purchaseorderdetailstermmap_ibfk_3` (`product`),
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderdetailstermmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderdetailstermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`podetails`) REFERENCES `podetails` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderdetailstermmap_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `mrpcontractdocmapping` (
`id`  varchar(40) NOT NULL ,
`mrpcontract`  varchar(40) NOT NULL ,
`documentid`  varchar(40) NOT NULL ,
`company`  varchar(40) NOT NULL ,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
KEY `FK_mrpcontractdocmapping_mrpcontract` (`mrpcontract`),
KEY `FK_mrpcontractdocmapping_documentid` (`documentid`),
KEY `FK_mrpcontractdocmapping_company` (`company`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdocmapping_mrpcontract` FOREIGN KEY (`mrpcontract`) REFERENCES `mrpcontract` (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdocmapping_documentid` FOREIGN KEY (`documentid`) REFERENCES `mrpcontractdoc` (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_mrpcontractdocmapping_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
)ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `machine_asset_mapping` (
`id`  varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
`machine`  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
`assetDetails`  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
`company`  varchar(255) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`machine`) REFERENCES `machine` (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`assetDetails`) REFERENCES `assetdetail` (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`))
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `machinemanratio` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `dateforratio` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `modifiedon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `createdby` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `modifiedby` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `machine` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `fullmachinetime` double DEFAULT '0',
  `fullmantime` double DEFAULT '0',
  `partmachinetime` double DEFAULT '0',
  `partmantime` double DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`machine`) REFERENCES `machine` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`createdby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `exciseInvoicedetails` (
`id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`goodsreceipt` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`supplier` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`suppliertinsalestaxno` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`supplierexciseregnno` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`cstnumber` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`supplierrange` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`suppliercommissionerate` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`supplieraddress` varchar(1024)  DEFAULT "",
`supplierstate` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`supplierimporterexportercode` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`supplierdivision` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturername` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerexciseregnno` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerrange` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturercommissionerate` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerdivision` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufactureraddress` varchar(1024)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerimporterexportercode` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufactureinvoiceno` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufactureinvoicedate` date DEFAULT NULL, 
PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`goodsreceipt`) REFERENCES `goodsreceipt` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
FOREIGN KEY (`supplierstate`) REFERENCES `state` (`id`)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

alter table workorder add seqnumber int(11) DEFAULT '0';
alter table workorder add datesuffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '';
alter table workorder add datepreffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '';
alter table workorder add autogen char(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'F';

alter table workcenter add seqnumber int(11) DEFAULT '0';
alter table workcenter add datesuffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '';
alter table workcenter add datepreffixvalue varchar(50) DEFAULT '';
alter table workcenter add autogen char(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'F';
alter table workcenter add CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_wcloaction` FOREIGN KEY (`workcenterlocation`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`);



CREATE TABLE `product_workcentre_mapping` (
`id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`productid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`workcentreid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`companyid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_prod_map_wcid` FOREIGN KEY (`workcentreid`) REFERENCES `workcenter` (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_prod_map_prodid` FOREIGN KEY (`productid`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_prod_map_compid` FOREIGN KEY (`companyid`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`) )ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `material_workcentre_mapping` (
`id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`materialid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
`workcentreid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
`companyid` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_bom_map_wcid` FOREIGN KEY (`workcentreid`) REFERENCES `workcenter` (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_bom_map_prodid` FOREIGN KEY (`materialid`) REFERENCES `bomdetail` (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_wc_bom_map_compid` FOREIGN KEY (`companyid`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`) )ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
